state 91

    (32) while_stmt_closed -> while_cond . closed_stmt
    (33) while_stmt_open -> while_cond . open_stmt
    (18) closed_stmt -> . simple_stmt
    (19) closed_stmt -> . while_stmt_closed
    (20) closed_stmt -> . for_stmt_closed
    (21) closed_stmt -> . if_stmt_closed
    (22) open_stmt -> . while_stmt_open
    (23) open_stmt -> . for_stmt_open
    (24) open_stmt -> . if_stmt_open
    (35) simple_stmt -> . error RBRACE
    (36) simple_stmt -> . error SEMICOLON
    (37) simple_stmt -> . expr SEMICOLON
    (38) simple_stmt -> . decl
    (39) simple_stmt -> . block_stmt
    (40) simple_stmt -> . continue_stmt
    (41) simple_stmt -> . break_stmt
    (42) simple_stmt -> . return_stmt
    (43) simple_stmt -> . print_stmt
    (32) while_stmt_closed -> . while_cond closed_stmt
    (29) for_stmt_closed -> . for_header closed_stmt
    (27) if_stmt_closed -> . if_cond closed_stmt ELSE closed_stmt
    (33) while_stmt_open -> . while_cond open_stmt
    (30) for_stmt_open -> . for_header open_stmt
    (25) if_stmt_open -> . if_cond stmt
    (26) if_stmt_open -> . if_cond closed_stmt ELSE if_stmt_open
    (60) expr -> . expr1
    (4) decl -> . decl_init
    (5) decl -> . ID COLON type_func SEMICOLON
    (6) decl -> . ID COLON type_array_sized SEMICOLON
    (7) decl -> . ID COLON type_simple SEMICOLON
    (52) block_stmt -> . LBRACE error RBRACE
    (53) block_stmt -> . LBRACE stmt_list RBRACE
    (50) continue_stmt -> . CONTINUE error
    (51) continue_stmt -> . CONTINUE SEMICOLON
    (48) break_stmt -> . BREAK error
    (49) break_stmt -> . BREAK SEMICOLON
    (46) return_stmt -> . RETURN opt_expr error
